  <span id="freeText7049696035841045568" style="display:none">I wrote a review for this on my blog, but since I wrote it right after I finished reading the book, I was on a bit of what I call a "book hangover." Yeah. Don't ask. It's crazy. So now that it's been 48 hours... I've calmed down and I'm going to attempt to write a spoiler-free review.<br /><br />If you're not afraid of a spoiler-crazy review, you can visit my blog and check out my <a href="http://leecheeeee813.blogspot.com/2011/01/ascend.html" rel="nofollow noopener">review</a>. <br /><br />I devoured the first two books as soon as I got them. I really liked them. I was just super excited for this one, and I was not disappointed. Mostly. The ending made me want to kill a couple of people (Not the very ending. It was happy.), because of a few romantic set ups. Anyways... before I start ranting again... <br /><br />The beginning was kind of surprising, because Loki just randomly showed up. Now, I've been having some mixed feelings about him. In no way whatsoever did he make them any better at the end. But yeah. He's kind of confusing, which I guess is good, but I still don't think he was explained enough. I mean, Wendy barely even knows him, and she just goes with what he says and trusts him completely. What???<br /><br />Wendy totally changed in this one. She went from being a shy girl that was all "I can't be a princess! What if I get everybody killed?" to "I am your Princess, so you do what I say. Got it? Good." It was so sudden, I liked it and didn't really like it at the same time. She just changed too much to like.<br /><br />Finn. I can't talk about him. Not without ruining it. All I can say is that I am Team Finn all the way. :)<br /><br />Elora changed in this one, too, but I liked it much more. I guess when you're on your death bed it does that to you (That's not a spoiler, right? I mean, she was sick since the second book...). She truly showed her love for Wendy, and it made me cry. I really felt for her and Wendy and wished that they could've had a normal mother-daughter relationship. Alas.<br /><br />Speaking of mothers, Sara isn't in this one much (or in any of them), but I really like her. I just wish she was more vocal rather than being a little follower Queen.<br /><br />I just love the other characters. They're such great people. I love Matt, and Willa, and Duncan. I wish they were my best friends. I miss Duncan's clumsiness. What happened to it???<br /><br />I think my biggest complaint would be how short this one was. I loved the book, I really hope there's more! (A spin-off, or two?) Also about how short it was- I think some parts were too rushed. I wish the battle was a little more interesting and descriptive, not just done with in two pages. <br /><br />I loved this book's action (There's more in this one. It keeps you on edge.) and humor (Wendy is so funny. I love her sarcasm.). I think I can compare this book to Twilight and The Hunger Games. Twilight because Wendy is like Bella with nothing short of a billion guys in her life and she has to choose one. The Hunger Games because, well, I can't get into it too much or else I'll spoil it, but let's just say I didn't exactly prefer the guys that Katniss and Wendy end up with. I was just a little pissed (Ok, maybe a little more than that... It's not like I'm mentally rewriting the ending. *scoffs* /sarcasm) ...<br /><br />Read this book! It has its twists and turns that I just totally inhaled and ended up with wanting more! This series introduced me to author Amanda Hocking, and I will definitely be looking for more of her books! </span>
  <a data-text-id="7049696035841045568" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/157138748" />
    <a title="Jennifer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4100360-jennifer"><img alt="Jennifer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1280838832p2/4100360.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/157138748?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/4100360-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/10203031-ascend">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4100360-jennifer?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4100360-jennifer?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer157138748" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13771971171952995842">Ascend is the perfect ending to the Trylle Trilogy. I'm sure there are more than a few people who wish Amanda Hocking had taken the obvious route with her plot, but I for one am so glad she didn't. <br/><br/>Wendy is trying to save her people but they continue to fight against her and amongst themselves making her task seem insurmountable. She has put the needs of her kingdom ahead of her own, but no matter what she tries, everything seems to be falling apart. I love that Wendy fights for what she believe</span>
  <span id="freeText13771971171952995842" style="display:none">Ascend is the perfect ending to the Trylle Trilogy. I'm sure there are more than a few people who wish Amanda Hocking had taken the obvious route with her plot, but I for one am so glad she didn't. <br /><br />Wendy is trying to save her people but they continue to fight against her and amongst themselves making her task seem insurmountable. She has put the needs of her kingdom ahead of her own, but no matter what she tries, everything seems to be falling apart. I love that Wendy fights for what she believes in, whether it is popular or not. She stands her ground and will not be swayed. <br /><br />The resolution of this novel is straightforward, but not as simple as it seems from the outset, and certainly not what I was expecting. It's marvelous that after getting to know Hocking's style she can continue to surprise and delight me with the artistry of her story telling. The relationships between her characters, from the major ones to the minor ones, are wonderful. I keep going back to them again and again because they are honest and true. <br /><br />This is a brilliant series and I look forward to starting the My Blood Approves series from her as well as any and all of her future endeavors. I'm thrilled about Amanda Hocking's recent successes and I wish her many more. <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://girlsjustreading.blogspot.com/2011/03/jenns-review-ascend.html">http://girlsjustreading.blogspot.com/...</a></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_557688764" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/557688764" />
    <a title="Madeleine Cleary" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9363651-madeleine-cleary"><img alt="Madeleine Cleary" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1491123366p2/9363651.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/557688764?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Madeleine Cleary" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Madeleine Cleary" href="/user/show/9363651-madeleine-cleary">Madeleine Cleary</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/10203031-ascend">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer557688764&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer557688764" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7048095954016384273">SPOILERS<br/><br/>I have so many problems with this book I don't know where to start.<br/><br/>Everything was FAR too convenient. They went to war and no one they knew died? How convenient. She fell in love with the Prince of the other kingdom they were at war with? How convenient!<br/><br/>In fact this book made me squirm the entire way throughout it. Not because it was any good either. The series as a whole was okay. It was very imaginative and interesting, steeped in folklore and magic. It has been compared with Harry Pot</span>
  <span id="freeText7048095954016384273" style="display:none">SPOILERS<br /><br />I have so many problems with this book I don't know where to start.<br /><br />Everything was FAR too convenient. They went to war and no one they knew died? How convenient. She fell in love with the Prince of the other kingdom they were at war with? How convenient!<br /><br />In fact this book made me squirm the entire way throughout it. Not because it was any good either. The series as a whole was okay. It was very imaginative and interesting, steeped in folklore and magic. It has been compared with Harry Potter, which is completely absurd.<br /><br />Firstly, why did the author bother to start up the whole Finn/Wendy relationship when nothing would happen? The readers fell in love with Finn. She said she loved him but then turned around and said 'you aren't trying hard enough'. What a pain in the arse she is! This guy comes from a poor family who depend upon him to bring in an income and has always been told to follow duty. Yet she expects him to just abandon his family and his duty and just be with her? What a fool he would be!<br /><br />Secondly, she slept with Loki while MARRIED to her HUSBAND? What kind of terrible morals is this author conveying? Oh but it was okay because her husband is gay and they don't actually love each other. NO! What a terrible way to start a relationship with Loki. Why would I as a reader like him if he is willing to do such a thing??<br /><br />Thirdly, the 'everything is happy' scene at the end made me feel sick. Life does not work out that way and the author is conveying a false reality. It's just so convenient that Finn found someone else to love. <br /><br />This last book made me seriously disappointed in the entire series.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7048095954016384273" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('w4/+gqJ+/gBteAgsyhr/ZgKwDMz1LLiaC9r6iOXAobwPv1y6w1fWllsRn7jrsgJX8vg2q4rfAHOj/GBBXTgEUg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('u9ef+ad3JkMvSXtUgkVQQuvhO4MyLGRJQrt1pdNne4B35z3Bxl4O1Rkg7MCj7a1zG6kB5E3f3KDqne9sa5/ebg==')})
  }

Her zombie series</span>
  <span id="freeText1835361004698377939" style="display:none">AMANDA HOCKING is the author of over twenty young adult novels, including the New York Times bestselling Trylle Trilogy and Kanin Chronicles. Her love of pop culture and all things paranormal influence her writing. She spends her time in Minnesota, taking care of her menagerie of pets and working on her next book.<br /><br />Several of her books have made the New York Times Bestsellers list. Her zombie series, <a href="http://www.hockingbooks.com/amanda-hockings-books/hollowland-series/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Hollows</a>, has been adapted into a graphic novel by Dynamite. She has published over twenty novels, including <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/48928-trylle&gt; the Trylle Trilogy&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a href=" rel="nofollow noopener">The Kanin Chronicles</a>, <a href="http://www.hockingbooks.com/amanda-hockings-books/watersong-series/" rel="nofollow noopener">the Watersong quartet</a>, <a href="http://www.hockingbooks.com/amanda-hockings-books/my-blood-approves-series/" rel="nofollow noopener">My Blood Approves series</a>, the Valkyrie duology<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/150484-valkyrie" rel="nofollow noopener"></a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25184362-freeks#other_reviews" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <em>Freeks</em>
</a>.<br /><br />Her next books are the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/47590299-the-lost-city" rel="nofollow noopener"> Omte Origins</a>, a trilogy set in the world of the Trylle and Kanin. The first book <em> The Lost City</em> will be out July 7, 2020, and the second book <em> The Morning Flower </em> will be out August 5, 2020. <br /><br />For more info about her and her books, here are some other places to check out and ways to contact her:<br /><br />Website: <a href="http://www.hockingbooks.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">www.hockingbooks.com</a><br /><br />Amazon Author Page: <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Amanda-Hocking/e/B003H4L762" rel="nofollow noopener">amazon.com/author/amandahocking</a><br /><br />Instagram: <a href="https://instagram.com/amanda_hocking/" rel="nofollow noopener">instagram.com/amanda_hocking/</a><br /><br />YouTube: <a href="https://www.youtube.com/aehocking" rel="nofollow noopener">www.youtube.com/aehocking</a><br /><br /><br />Pinterest: <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/aehocking/" rel="nofollow noopener">www.pinterest.com/aehocking/</a><br /></span>
